# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

## #1

- Gear: Baggy
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Legs
- Color: Green
- Stat Buffs
    - Armor ✦ = Lx1.25
    - Kernel Slots = L
    - Initiative = L
    - Speed = D+1
    - Movement Speed = Lx2
- Actives:
    - [Healing Touch](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Healing+Touch)
    - [Thorns](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Thorns)
    - You have access to Tiers I-IV of each of your Actives.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

## #772

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: AOE Buff
    - Your AOE Radius now = Perception x2.5
    - Your AOEs now get a +7 Damage Plus.
    - You can exclude anyone you want from your AOEs.
    - Three times a turn you can either push everyone who got hit by an AOE attack to the tiles right beyond your AOE Radius or pull them as close as they can be to the center of your AOE.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Ydilikian (Medieval)
